Song Ziwen Discusses Plans After Abolishing Likin 74

Unified Tax and Special Taxes Unified as Central Revenue

Tax Bureau Staff Transferred from Customs Chinese Staff to Fill Positions

Tianjin Correspondence: Minister of Finance Song Ziwen came to Tianjin to discuss subsidy tax measures after the abolition of likin with Zhang Xueliang and the northern authorities. Yesterday (the 9th), he spoke with Zhang and financial personnel for a long time. A reporter visited Song today, and according to Mr. Song's account, the general outline of all the facilities after the abolition of likin is as follows:

Mr. Song first stated that he had not been to the north for more than two years. The finances of the northern provinces have been very chaotic after the war, so he came to inspect them in person and meet with Deputy Commander Zhang and financial personnel to discuss all measures after the abolition of likin. Rumors that he came here for the post-war settlement of the Northwest and the disbandment expenses of the Northwest armies are actually incorrect. The Northwest issue is handled directly by Commanders-in-Chief Jiang and Zhang, and does not require his participation. The subsidy tax after the abolition of likin in the north will be implemented in accordance with the methods stipulated by the central government. However, how to establish bureaus for collection, and where to set up tax bureaus for collecting certain goods, can only be decided after investigation. Deputy Commander Zhang is very decisive in implementing the abolition of likin. Seeing his telegram urging the northern provinces to implement it, such revolutionary measures are admirable. The income from subsidy taxes after the abolition of likin in the northern provinces still cannot make up for the original amount, and the difference will be subsidized by the central government. Currently, all provinces across the country have uniformly complied with the order to abolish likin, and their replies have all arrived at the ministry. The subsidy tax collection method is also uniformly handled in accordance with the provisions of the central government. The subsidy tax consists of two types: unified tax and special consumption tax. The unified tax is levied on five types: cigarettes, wheat flour, matches, cement, and cotton yarn. The first two types have been levied for a long time, and the three types currently being levied are relatively easy to handle. Personnel can be dispatched to the place of production to collect taxes. The tax items listed in the consumption tax are nineteen types. The outside world often misunderstands that with so many tax items, its harshness is not far from likin. In fact, this is not the case, because in implementation, bureaus are set up to collect taxes on major products based on the production conditions of each region. Not every province sets up tax bureaus one by one according to the items listed in the tax items. Therefore, in practice, the tax to be levied in each province is only three or five items. Taxes cannot be levied in areas where they are not produced. In summary, that is, for one type of goods, no matter where it is located, those who have paid taxes can circulate throughout the country without being taxed again. One item, one tax. Those who collect cocoons will no longer collect silk. However, after the abolition of likin, the finances of both the central and local governments are very difficult, and the people should understand this. The soaring price of gold has also made the national economy very difficult, and the central government should carefully consider the gains and losses and formulate new tax rules. The new tax rules for consumption tax and business tax have been submitted by the ministry to the Legislative Yuan for review and promulgation. The reporter asked what would be used as the basis for collection before the new tax was promulgated. Song replied that there may be a slight pause during this period. Some outsiders have criticized us for abolishing likin rashly without sufficient preparation in advance, not knowing that if everything is considered and discussed calmly, there will never be a day for implementation. Therefore, we had to implement it resolutely with the means of cutting the Gordian knot. The reporter also asked how the central and local finances would be divided in the future. Song replied that business tax and stamp tax are local revenue, while unified tax and special consumption tax are central revenue. When local government expenses are insufficient, they will be subsidized by the central government. The Unified Tax Bureau and the Special Tax Bureau are directly under the Ministry of Finance. Before the financial commissioners are abolished, they are supervised by the commissioners. After they are abolished, they are supervised by the Tax Affairs Administration and the Customs Administration. The personnel required by the tax bureaus are all transferred from various customs Chinese staff to fill the positions. Those who are insufficient will be recruited through examinations. The recruited personnel will have a probationary period of six months, and will be awarded positions based on their performance after the period expires. The reason for transferring customs Chinese staff is that they have been trained and are familiar with the rules. After the transfer, the preferential conditions they received in the customs will still be maintained. The appointment service rules and preferential treatment methods for tax bureau staff will also be formulated in accordance with customs precedents. The failure of the likin system was mostly caused by the staff of the likin bureaus. Whenever a new director is appointed, the staff will be changed accordingly, leading to acts of greed and dereliction of duty. After the system is reformed, this malpractice can be swept away. The reporter asked whether the 60 million yuan cigarette public bond has been issued and whether it will be used as a subsidy after the abolition of likin. Song replied that the bonds are still being issued, but not to compensate for the loss of likin. The disbandment of the army and the payment of salaries to the armies attached to the Second Group are all paid from this fund. When asked whether there have been any contacts with foreign countries who are willing to lend money to our country, Song said that the United States is willing to lend money to our country because it has a surplus of domestic silver production. Lending to our country is a way for them to save themselves and does not benefit our country much. When asked whether it is true that regular customs within fifty miles still collect export goods tax, Song said that since the implementation of the new tariff, there have been fewer foreign goods coming in and exports are not very prosperous, so it is being collected temporarily. When asked whether the minister had discussed with Chairman Yan the issue of Shanxi's plan to issue post-war public bonds, which was previously rejected by the central government, Song said that this is one of the Northwest issues and is under the control of Deputy Commander Zhang, and he has no need to contact Chairman Yan. The issuance of public bonds is a major issue and should be considered carefully. When asked whether Chairman Jiang intends to come to the north or go to Shaanxi, Song said that Chairman Jiang is very busy with government affairs and may not be able to spare time for a while. It is heard that Mr. Song will stay in Tianjin for two or three days and will not go to Shenyang. (January 10)

Jiangxi Province's Finances After Abolishing Likin 75

Local Annual Income Short by 1.7 Million

Education Treasury Bond Fund Also Not Secured

All Levels of Agencies Reduce Staff and Streamline Administration

Nanchang Correspondence: After the Jiangxi Provincial Government was ordered to abolish likin, it immediately submitted the matter to the 340th provincial affairs meeting and the tenth temporary meeting on New Year's Eve for discussion and implementation. It was resolved that: (1) A reply to the central government should be submitted, and the abolition of likin should be strictly implemented, and a telegram should be sent to support the central government's abolition of likin. (2) The likin in this province had already been classified as Jiangxi's revenue by the central government's standard for dividing national and local taxes, and the Jiangxi Financial Commissioner should be instructed to implement its abolition. (3) Various local taxes similar to likin should be immediately ordered by the Finance Department to investigate and abolish them separately, and alternative subsidies should be planned and submitted for approval. Currently, various special tax bureaus and consumption tax bureaus in Jiangxi Province were closed on New Year's Eve last year. In the past, the Nancun Municipal Special Tax, Jiangxi Autonomous Special Tax, and 55% surtax on cigarettes and alcohol attached to likin have all been abolished. Recently, Huang Bozhong, member of the Provincial Committee and Director of the Finance Department, proposed to the provincial government that the taxes and levies in Jiangxi Province similar to likin have been abolished in accordance with the Ministry's telegram. It is estimated that local income will be reduced by 970,000 yuan annually. The livestock tax is currently being consulted with the Ministry of Finance for a reply. If it also needs to be abolished, the annual local revenue will be reduced by more than 1.8 million yuan. However, the revenue from the business tax, in addition to offsetting the original tooth tax of 100,000 yuan, is only 100,000 yuan in actual income. The statistical deficit is more than 1.7 million yuan. It seems that the provincial government should transfer to the Ministry of Finance in accordance with the provisions of Item C of the Yuan Decree, and allocate the funds for subsidies to maintain the current financial situation in Jiangxi Province so that local administration will not be interrupted. It is heard that the provincial government has decided to send members Xiong Yuxi and Chen Zanyu, director of the Salt Transport Bureau, to Beijing to ask Chairman Jiang and Finance Minister Song for instructions on subsidy measures. In addition, the salt tax has been classified as central revenue, and local surcharges on salt have also been abolished. This item is also a major source of revenue for Jiangxi, amounting to about 5 million yuan annually, and is designated for education funds and repayment of treasury bond funds. Since it has been abolished, the education treasury bond fund has been fundamentally shaken. Each treasury bond of one yuan is now worth less than the South Corner, and the education sector is sending letters and telegrams asking for remedies because education funds are not secured. The Provincial Education Federation has also telegraphed to request Director Jiang of the Education Department, who is inspecting Yiyang, to return to the province to properly plan measures. The Education Department has also sent Section Chief Deng to Beijing to ask for instructions on everything. It is found that the finances of this province are due to the fact that the communist bandits are all over the territory, and the income is less than two-tenths of the budget, resulting in arrears of several million yuan in political expenses. Various agencies have not been paid for four or five months. The solar New Year's Eve already feels like the end of the road, and the circulating coupons have fallen to 80%, and the common people are crying out in pain. After the abolition of likin, the difficulties can be imagined. Currently, the Finance Department, in addition to sending people everywhere to collect grain, all agencies have adopted a tight policy, reducing staff and streamlining administration. Even the municipal government, due to the abolition of municipal donations, has reduced its administration by two-thirds and laid off many employees. The rest of the agencies will also carry out large-scale layoffs and pay cuts. Public officials are all in danger of being dismissed. (January 12)

Zhang Xueliang Discusses China's Peaceful Unification and East Asia 76

Shenyang Correspondence: In response to a request from the Osaka Mainichi Shimbun of Japan, Deputy Commander Zhang Xueliang wrote an article entitled "China's Peaceful Unification and East Asia" before the Lunar New Year, which was published in the newspaper's New Year's Day special issue in the 20th year of the Republic of China. Readers can see Zhang's latest views on the domestic and international situation. The original text is recorded below:

"At the end of the 19th year of the Republic of China, a reporter from the Osaka Mainichi Shimbun of Japan asked for a preface for the New Year's Day supplement. The letters were frequent, and I could not elaborate. Let me briefly describe what I have been thinking about in response. Since the Republic of China, there have been frequent turmoil and disorder in the political situation. It is not enough to revive itself internally, and it does not benefit friendly countries externally. It has only burdened itself with failures, and I am very ashamed of it. This is not to mention. However, national turmoil is something that should be experienced in the process of political evolution. In this process, it is impossible to be completely perfect in handling internal and external affairs. What can be comforting is that our people, who are in the midst of glory and decline, have never changed their integrity of peace and honesty. Although they are gentle, they do not eat others. Although they are strong, they do not spit others out. Even in this process of turmoil, those who seek peace and eliminate chaos have always been consistent. The completion of this unification took less than ten days. Xue Liang's clever telegram was only an occasional trigger. The centripetal force and love that have been accumulated and condensed still come from the people's self-awareness. It is by no means something that can be done by one hand or one foot. For example, the central government did not make excessive demands when the peace talks were first concluded, but showed leniency. Yan and Feng did not fight to the bitter end, but stopped fighting on their own. All of this is enough to prove that the root of peace of our people is deeply rooted in people's hearts. Although the disputes between brothers may occasionally undergo changes, the clear waves and autumn waters will eventually lead to tranquility. Is it not a generous measure and a common creation? Is the virtue of humility the same as the original nature?

Moreover, looking at the historical examples of China and the West, the cause of governance and peace cannot be separated from armor and soldiers. Only Mencius has the saying that those who do not like to kill people can unite the world. However, it is only a theoretical suspension, thousands of years away. He actually fulfilled his previous words. Peaceful unification is really a precedent. If we can expand this path, then the way to attract peace and pacify the world is not only to make up for the previous shortcomings, but also to be the initial foundation of the Great Harmony. Japan and China are separated by a strip of water, dependent on each other. Those who share the same race, the same script, the same politics, and the same religion have been around for thousands of years. Therefore, their feelings of love are not very far apart. The friendship of sharing weal and woe should also be more important than other countries. Now that China has initially unified the world and a grand foundation has just been opened, we should work together to achieve prosperity. As a brotherly country, Japan is close in affection and adjacent in territory. The so-called congratulation of the emperor's crown and the congratulation of neighbors are naturally very different from ordinary people. Moreover, the lips and teeth are closely connected, and the interests are shared. Politics, education, and culture are closely connected. What is especially needed and cannot be separated is the issue of supply and demand between the two countries.

In general, China's exports are mostly necessary for Japan, and the sales of Japanese industries are concentrated in China. Therefore, China's governance and chaos, prosperity and decline are related to Japan. Assuming that from now on, China's fields and products will become more abundant day by day, its supply and demand from Japan will be boundless, and Japan's national wealth will gradually increase. If, on the contrary, there is continuous turmoil and all industries are depressed, then it will be reversed. The shortage of Japanese commodities and raw materials will directly affect people's livelihood and indirectly affect its national power. This is evidenced by the fact that the decline in silver prices this year has affected the business districts of neighboring countries, which is even more obvious. Therefore, China's peace invisibly guarantees Japan's prosperity. The prosperity of China and Japan will enable East Asia to maintain its safety. This key is not very related to any political or cultural issues. In short, economic conditions are the key to the mutual needs and shared prosperity of the two countries, and this key is not something that both parties can have on their own. It must be achieved with a corresponding attitude of mutual assistance, and it cannot be maintained without failure. This is what Xue Liang dares to firmly believe. In terms of the current world situation, various places in Asia are very easy to become the focus of contention among various countries. After the European War, scholars often regarded one end of China as the second Balkan Peninsula, which is enough to cause the world to be uneasy again. Although their words may not be very accurate, and whether or not they are willing to be slaughtered depends on themselves, the seriousness of the East Asian issue seems to be undeniable. Therefore, to achieve world peace, the first step should be to seek it in East Asia. How to realize and maintain East Asian peace depends on whether Japan and China can implement friendship. The so-called friendship is not in verbal propaganda, but in actual performance. The past gaps and constraints between the two countries, as well as the future doubts and obstacles, should be frankly believed and permanently resolved. I hope that people from both countries will further ensure their mutual stability and bear the responsibility for peace in East Asia. This is not only for the benefit of East Asia, but also for the needs of the world. This is also the sincere hope of Xue Liang for the efforts of the sages of both countries." (9th)

Handling of Counter-Revolutionary Suspects in Bengbu 77

Communist Shi Yuyao Escorted to Headquarters for Interrogation

Other Arrested Persons Temporarily Released on Bail

Bengbu Correspondence: Last month, the Bengbu military police successively arrested 14 suspected counter-revolutionaries at the Second Provincial Rural Normal School in Bengshan, Bengbu. After an interrogation by the military law office of the Anhui North Garrison Headquarters, the arrested Dean of Studies Hou Mengxuan, Dean of Student Affairs Xie Juemin, and others confessed that only the actions of students Shi Yuyao and Yang Chonghan seemed suspicious. On December 11, the anniversary of the Communist Party's riot in Guangzhou, Shi and Yang went out without asking for leave and did not return until late. In addition, they requested the issuance of uniforms and incited a wave of unrest. When the military police inspected, Shi Yuyao burned books in the kitchen. The military judge then brought Shi Yuyao and Yang Chonghan for questioning. The two firmly refused to confess and were sent back to prison. Garrison Commander Shu Lihuang, in order to get to the bottom of the matter, ordered Jiang Yangzheng, director of the military law office, to go to the school with the military judge and adjutant to investigate. After two investigations, and verifying the opinions of all parties, it was confirmed that Shi Yuyao was indeed suspected of being a counter-revolutionary. The military law office checked the case file of the communist Shen Chaoxian, which was presented by Song Shike, commander of the Third Detachment, and found letters from Jiang Yigong (aka Jiang Chuanzheng) and Jiang Mengping (aka Jiang Chuanhe), students of the Second Rural Normal School, to Shen.

Page 10

In the middle, Shi Yuyao also added his own words. After the investigation was completed, Shi Yuyao was interrogated five more times, and the evidence and documents obtained from the investigation were proved one by one. After repeated rebuttals, he finally did not deny it. Shi confessed to joining the Communist Party and taking on propaganda work, and confessed that he was introduced into the party by Ding Zhengfang from Liu'an. Ding was short and stocky, with a face full of pimples, and his hair was pointed. He was about 20 years old. He also personally wrote three reports (the text is very long and contains words of wishing to repent). The garrison headquarters, believing that Shi had confessed to joining the Communist Party, presented Shi and the entire case file to the Nanjing Headquarters for interrogation a few days ago. As for the Communist Party member Ding Zhengfang, who was confessed, he has been separately ordered to be wanted. The other people, such as Hou Mengxuan, Xie Juemin, Wang Baosheng, Yang Chonghan, Zhu Wenhao, Tong Xiemin, Zhou Guangmo, Xu Zenglin, Cheng Xiangfu, Weng Fenglan, and Zhan Zhao, were interrogated repeatedly, but no suspicion was found. They have all been temporarily released on bail, pending the handling of the headquarters. However, Jiang Chuanzheng and Jiang Chuanhe are still being held in the garrison headquarters. Whether they are suspected or not will be determined after a clear investigation. (January 9)

British Economic Investigation Group Arrives in Hankou 78

Hankou Correspondence: The British Far East Economic Investigation Group, which came to China to investigate commerce, arrived in Beijing last month, and then went north to Liaoning. The group members Sir Alan, Greening, Dax, and Nais, after traveling from Liaoning to Tianjin, transferred by train south and arrived in Beijing on the 3rd of this month. They changed to the Ruhe wheel and came to Hankou with Mr. Mir, the British Consul in Ningbo. They arrived at the wharf at 3 pm on the 9th. The Hankou Municipal Government sent Pang Shengzhong, chief of the Fourth Section of the Secretariat, together with representatives from the General Chamber of Commerce, the Bankers Association, the Landlords Association, the Cotton Industry Association, and the United Yarn Factory Association, as well as British Consul General in Hankou, Mr. Balang, and overseas Chinese businessmen, to welcome them at the wharf. The British Overseas Chinese Chamber of Commerce held a special banquet on the afternoon of the 10th and invited local commercial leaders to accompany them. After the banquet, Alan and others took cars to inspect the Hankou riverside and prosperous streets for a week. The Hankou Municipal Government, the General Chamber of Commerce, the Bankers Association, the Landlords Association, the Cotton Industry Association, the United Yarn Factory Association, and other organizations held a banquet at the Bankers Association on the 11th to discuss opinions on Sino-British trade. The tour schedule was also set to start on the 11th, visiting the First Yarn Factory and major factories in Wuhan. On the 12th, they visited the Hankou Municipal Government, the Jianghan Customs, the Commodity Inspection Bureau, and the Salt Affairs Audit Office. On the 13th, they rested. On the 14th, they left Hankou and returned to Shanghai. According to Sir Alan, a member of the group, the investigation in China was briefly as follows: "Our group came to China purely to investigate your country's commerce in order to seek mutual development between China and the United Kingdom. After arriving in Shanghai in December last year, we immediately entered Beijing and went to the Northeast Provinces and Tianjin for investigation. We were very satisfied along the way. Currently, eight members of the group, including Sir Thomas, are still staying in the Northeast Provinces and will go to Shanghai in the next few days. We can only stay in Hankou for a few days. On the 27th, we will go to Hong Kong from Shanghai with Thomas and others, and return to the country via Canada. After our group returns to the country, we will strive for mutual development in commerce between the two countries." (January 10)

Plans for Suppressing Bandits and Purifying the Countryside in Henan 79

Proposed by Liu Zhenhua and Li Mingzhong

Draft Outline of the Plan for Suppressing Bandits and Purifying the Countryside to be Implemented in Henan Province by Liu Zhenhua and Li Mingzhong: (1) For this bandit suppression and countryside purification, it is proposed to divide each county in the entire province into districts and implement them simultaneously. Major bandit gangs will be the responsibility of the military to suppress, while scattered small bandits will be the responsibility of the county magistrate to supervise and order the police and militias to eliminate. At the same time, countryside purification will be implemented simultaneously with the suppression of bandit gangs and the elimination of scattered bandits to eliminate the source of bandits. (Explanation) Bandit suppression is a temporary measure, while countryside purification is a fundamental solution. The two are mutually necessary and dependent and should be implemented immediately without interruption. Simply suppressing bandits without purifying the countryside is not enough to eliminate the source of bandits. If countryside purification is not implemented immediately during bandit suppression, or if it is not carried out simultaneously in all counties of the province, then they will simply flee from one place to another, making it difficult to eradicate them completely. Therefore, this article places special emphasis on simultaneous implementation throughout the province to achieve complete success. (2) The military's bandit suppression areas will be divided based on the situation of bandit strongholds and the necessities of military operations. Remaining scattered bandits and countryside purification areas will be divided into four districts based on the old circuits. (Explanation) Military bandit suppression is a special operation for temporary treatment, so it seems appropriate to divide the area according to the needs of the situation to facilitate it. As for the elimination of scattered bandits, countryside purification, and the general operation throughout the province, it seems appropriate to utilize the interconnectedness of the county boundaries and the customary cooperation in defense and suppression over the years to achieve cooperative results. Therefore, it is proposed to use the old circuits as the areas. (3) All matters related to the division of bandit suppression areas and the allocation of troops shall be presided over and convened by the director of the Kaifeng Field Headquarters, with the resident Henan pacification supervisors and military officers meeting to formulate specific regulations, and each shall be responsible for suppression within their respective areas. (4) All matters related to the division of countryside purification areas and the handling of countryside purification shall be handled by the chairman of the Henan Provincial Government, who will make overall plans and notify the responsible officers and pacification supervisors to consult with the chairman and supervise the implementation within their respective areas. (Explanation) According to the provisions of Article 6 of the Countryside Purification Regulations, the director-general of the Countryside Purification Bureau in each province shall be concurrently held by the chairman of each province. Also, according to the provisions of Article 7 of the Provisional Organization Regulations of the Pacification Supervisor's Office, countryside purification matters shall be implemented by each supervisor in consultation with the provincial government to supervise its subordinates. Hence, the proposal of this article. (5) All troops that do not participate in bandit suppression shall be transferred by the director of the Field Headquarters to suitable locations for training. (6) The director of the Field Headquarters shall strictly prohibit all troops stationed in Henan from hiring or appeasing bandits. (7) The bandit suppression strategy shall focus on encircling and exterminating them. When encountering fleeing bandits who must be pursued, the director of the Field Headquarters shall notify the officers in charge of bandit suppression in each area and the troops in neighboring provinces to intercept them separately, regardless of jurisdictional boundaries. (8) The methods for joint military suppression and the regulations for police and militia cooperation in suppression, arrest, and defense shall be formulated separately by the director and the chairman and shall be notified to all bandit suppression troops and ordered to all county magistrates. (Explanation) The bandit gangs' entrenchment and the scattered bandits' escape often exploit gaps at the junctions of areas to evade capture. It is insufficient to prevent their spread without emphasizing the joint suppression by the military and the coordinated actions of the police and militias. Therefore, it is specifically requested to clearly define the joint suppression methods and various regulations for application. (9) In addition to handling the organization of the countryside purification organs in accordance with the Countryside Purification Regulations, it is proposed to establish several inspection commissioners within the General Bureau, divided by district, stationed in suitable locations in each district, to promptly supervise and inspect the areas where bandit gangs are entrenched. The provincial government may also allocate several countryside purification commissioners to each bandit suppression troop so that they can immediately promote countryside purification after bandit suppression to avoid delays. (Explanation) After the bandit gangs are eliminated, the military's power should be used to immediately foster local righteousness and expedite urgent tasks in countryside purification, such as searching for escaped bandits, inspecting firearms, and investigating household registrations. The situation in areas where bandit gangs are entrenched is different from that in other ordinary counties. Relying solely on the county magistrate to concurrently handle these matters amidst his busy schedule is insufficient to meet the urgent needs. It seems appropriate for the provincial government to allocate several experienced personnel to each troop to supervise the local officials and gentry to implement them diligently to avoid perfunctory and dilatory practices. (10) In addition to handling the procedures for implementing countryside purification in accordance with the Countryside Purification Regulations, it is proposed to pay special attention to dissolving all improper local organizations through persuasion and coercion, as stipulated in Article 25 of the original regulations. Furthermore, the province's security regiments should be organized in accordance with the county security regiment regulations. (Explanation) The province's countryside purification methods, such as investigating household registrations, implementing mutual guarantee and joint responsibility among neighbors, inspecting firearms, and handling funding, rewards, and punishments, have been clearly defined in the Countryside Purification Regulations and will not be repeated here. However, it has been found that there are numerous small, improper organizations in various counties, such as various types of heretical societies, whose situations are pitiful. Not only are they unable to defend themselves, but they also cause chaos. Special attention should be paid to dissolving them properly through persuasion and coercion to eliminate the source of chaos. As for the province's security regiments, they have been repeatedly reorganized and utilized by the stationed troops in recent years, resulting in inconsistent organization and numerous abuses. They have not been guided onto the right track. It now seems appropriate to strictly adhere to the National Government's county security regiment law, reorganize them, and implement the method of joint guarantees by squad leaders and joint guarantees by all households in the same squad to establish a foundation for social stability. (11) When implementing countryside purification and registering household populations, it is proposed to simultaneously compile autonomous regions such as districts, townships, towns, neighborhoods, and villages in accordance with the County Organization Law, as stipulated in Article 19 of the Countryside Purification Regulations, to assist in the implementation of political tutelage. (Explanation) It seems that this countryside purification should be truly implemented. When investigating household registrations, the various levels of autonomous regions should be compiled simultaneously in accordance with the County Organization Law to achieve a permanent solution and establish a reference for future implementation of political tutelage. This is the first fundamental plan for governing Henan. According to the provisions of Article 2 of the County Organization Implementation Law, Henan Province should complete county organization by August of the 19th year. However, military affairs have repeatedly arisen in recent years, resulting in delays. Now that military affairs have been resolved, it is possible to take advantage of this large-scale countryside purification to carry it out incidentally so that it can be completed as soon as possible and avoid the labor of repeating it in the future. It seems to be the same as the work of conscription and rewards. (12) The Provincial Government shall formulate methods for handling the surrender of bandits who surrender their weapons to avoid death and the surrender of innocent people who have been coerced, and shall properly formulate separate regulations for post-disaster relief and resettlement in areas severely affected by bandits and for recruiting refugees to resume new cultivation and implement them separately. (13) The Provincial Government shall write and disseminate popular propaganda to arouse the public's sympathy and assistance for bandit suppression and countryside purification. Publications that persuade various types of heretical societies shall also be widely compiled and disseminated to awaken the confused and stubborn. In order to increase the efficiency of bandit suppression and countryside purification, appropriate deadlines for bandit suppression and countryside purification shall be formulated separately with reference to the regulations and taking into account local conditions for joint compliance. (January 7)

The Third Day of the Jiangsu Province Pacification Conference 80

Discussion of Five Groups of Proposals Completed

Closing Ceremony Held Immediately

The Jiangsu Province Pacification Conference continued at 9:00 AM on the 12th at the Yangzhou Supervisor's Office. A total of 42 people attended, and 6 people attended as observers. Zhang Zhijiang first led the entire group in holding a memorial week, and then the presidium chairman Ma Yinbing chaired the discussion of the proposals as follows: A. Search and Suppression Group: (1) The Supervisor's Office proposed that countryside purification and search and suppression must be carried out simultaneously, and it is proposed to urgently implement rewards and punishments to invigorate the decadent and show encouragement. Resolved: Passed. (2) Proposed method for implementing the surrender of bandits. Resolved: Passed in principle. The surrender regulations will be submitted to the General Headquarters for approval after they are finalized before implementation. (3) Zhenjiang County proposed that the Supervisor's Office's subordinate teams be drawn to be stationed in Zhenjiang Shangdang Baoyan Gaozi and other places to prevent and suppress bandit disasters in order to strengthen provincial defenses and secure people's homes. (4) Jiangning County proposed to eliminate bandits in Maoshan Jiufeng Mountain and along the Yangtze River. The two cases were merged and resolved: The Security Department will allocate considerable troops nearby to be stationed in Shangdang and other places to engage in prevention and suppression. (5) Zhenjiang County proposed that the Supervisor's Office's subordinate teams each form guerrilla squads to supervise the local security regiments to search bandit dens at any time in order to purify the source of bandits. Resolved: Each county shall specially report to the Supervisor's Office to designate appropriate troops to assist the county magistrate in handling matters when needed. (6) Rugao County proposed that the pacification policy should focus on Xuzhou and Huai'an in order to purify the source of bandits and avoid their proliferation. Resolved: Handed over to the Supervisor's Office for handling. (7) Rugao County proposed that Jiangyin should be pacified in order to cut off the source of bandit weapons. Resolved: The Supervisor's Office shall order the port water and land police teams to strictly search to prevent the source, and shall also inform the Shanghai Municipal Government to order a uniform ban. (8) Rugao County proposed that the sea area should be pacified in order to maintain the livelihood of fishermen. (9) The Jiangsu Agricultural Department proposed to join the Civil Affairs Department and the Security Department to find ways to eliminate pirates and protect fishermen. The two cases were merged and resolved: The Supervisor's Office will join the Provincial Government in requesting the General Headquarters to allocate the navy to assist in the suppression within a time limit. (10) Xiaoxian County proposed to allocate a part of the troops directly under the Pacification Supervisor's Office to be stationed at the junction of Jiangsu, Anhui, and Henan provinces to eliminate bandit gangs on the border so that the local area can be permanently relieved of pain. Resolved: Passed in principle. (11) Jurong County proposed that the pacification troops should choose to be stationed in key areas after the search and suppression in order to facilitate the holding of countryside purification. Resolved: Passed in principle. (12) Liang Guanying proposed that bandit suppression should concentrate forces. Resolved: The Supervisor's Office will handle the matter according to the reports of the counties regarding how to allocate bandit suppression forces. (13) Liang Guanying proposed that the Provincial Government should be requested to issue a notice to the local authorities under its jurisdiction to actively assist the bandit suppression troops. Resolved: Passed. (14) Funing County proposed to set up shallow-water naval vessels for the Huaihai River to replace the water police sentinel ships for water and land patrol. Resolved: The counties concerned should jointly submit a special report to the Provincial Government for handling. (15) Baoying County proposed that before the establishment of the salt farm Gao Bao Huai Xing six counties' dike water patrol team, troops should be allocated to be stationed in the important passes along the dike to prevent blockage. Resolved: Passed. (16) Suqian County proposed that the stationed troops should be ordered to assist the local administrative officers in handling countryside purification. Resolved: Merged with the Countryside Purification Group for discussion. (17) Suqian County proposed that the 95th Brigade should be stationed in Suqian for a long time to eliminate bandits. Resolved: If the county needs it, the county magistrate should submit a special report to the Supervisor's Office for approval. (18) Suqian County proposed that the bandits captured in Jiangbei should still be handled in accordance with the previous bandit suppression regulations. Resolved: Merged with other groups for discussion. B. Countryside Purification Group: (1) Tongshan County proposed that the Xuzhou's Fengxiao Tongpei and five counties' joint defense zone should expedite the countryside purification. Resolved: Passed. The Provincial Government will forward it to the five counties to expedite the handling. (2) Jiangsu Evening News suggested that the gentry who reward countryside purification should be rewarded. Resolved: Passed. The specific regulations will be sent to the Provincial Government for formulation and implementation. (3) Jingjiang County proposed to formulate methods for purchasing civilian-held firearms and regulations for punishing those who hide them without reporting. Resolved: Seriously inspect civilian-held firearms, no need to buy them. Those who hide them without reporting shall be treated as privately storing military firearms. C. Self-Defense Group: (1) Tongshan County proposed that the security regiments of each county should be thoroughly reorganized and trained in order to strengthen the public's military force and eliminate bandit disasters. Resolved: Passed. D. Post-Disaster Group: (1) The Construction Department proposed to request the Supervisor's Office to draw troops to dig out the shallow sections of the Li Canal in order to help farmers and enrich people's lives. Resolved: The method of drawing soldiers to dig out the shallow sections of the Li Canal is very good. However, whether the pacification troops can be drawn should be determined by the Supervisor's Office and then discussed with the Construction Department. (2) The Agriculture and Mines Department proposed to carry out land reclamation to eliminate salt bandits and pacify Jiangbei. (3) It also proposed to make suggestions for pacification and post-disaster and request public decision to assist in the progress. The two cases were merged and resolved: Regarding the reclamation of land by soldiers, this is a fundamental method to eliminate the source of bandits. However, this matter is of great importance, and the Supervisor's Office should be requested to join the Provincial Government in formulating regulations and organizing a pacification and post-disaster committee to discuss in detail. As for planning the establishment of branches of the Farmers' Bank, promoting the operation of cooperatives, promoting new agricultural tools, and distributing superior seedlings, the Supervisor's Office should be requested to order its subordinates to be responsible for protection and assist in the promotion at any time. E. Other Groups: (1) The Supervisor's Office proposed to pacify the Taihu Lake area. (2) Wuxian County proposed that bandits have been harming the Taihu Lake and other places for a long time, and military institutions should be established on the east and west mountains of Dongting to be responsible for prevention and suppression, and to surround the bandit areas on all sides to eliminate them in one fell swoop. The two cases were merged and resolved: Passed in principle. The detailed method will be discussed and handled by the Supervisor's Office and the Provincial Government.

After the proposals were resolved, the closing ceremony was held at 6:00 PM that evening. Zhang Zhijiang delivered the closing speech, and Hu Pu'an, the director of the Civil Affairs Department, also gave a speech. After the speeches, the meeting was adjourned.

Local Communications

Suzhou 81

The candidate for the president of the Wuxi County Court has been determined. The High Court was ordered to prepare for the establishment of the Wuxi County Court. The site and buildings of the court were built in December last year. The establishment was delayed because the internal layout was not completed and the position of president was not determined. Yesterday, President Lin received an order from the Ministry that the position of president of the Xixian County Court would be filled by Guo Shouyi, the current presiding judge of the Shanghai Local Court. The date of establishment is approximately the 20th of this month, and the office will open on February 1st.

The perpetrators of the Du Wu assassination case were escorted to the province. In November last year, the third district of the Water Public Security Bureau successively arrested six bandits Luo Daosheng, Peng Zufu, Jiang Zhaofu, Li Desheng, Xiong San, and He Yuzhang, who assassinated Du Wu, the squad leader of the 14th Team, 1st Squad. After District Magistrate Shen Weikun interrogated them and obtained clear confessions, he submitted them to the Provincial Department for review. On the previous day (12th), District Magistrate Shen received instructions from the Department of Civil Affairs, ordering the six key criminals Luo Daosheng, etc., who were arrested for the Du assassination case, to be escorted to the Provincial Security Department for review. After District Magistrate Shen received the order, he sent staff to escort Luo Daosheng, etc., to the province at 9:00 a.m. yesterday to await their fate.

Wounded soldiers who have recovered are sent to Beijing to return to their teams. The 15th and 17th wounded soldiers hospitals in Su-di have already been merged. At 11:00 a.m. yesterday (13th), the 17th Rear Hospital in Tiger Hill sent 153 wounded soldiers who had recovered to Beijing to return to their teams.

Why was Zhang Huifen assassinated? Zhang Wenqing's (a partner in Nanying Futaiyuan Paint Store) daughter Huifen was at No. 22, Zhijia Inn, outside Gusu Gate, when two unknown men knocked on the door at 7:00 p.m. on the previous day (12th), entered the house, and stabbed Huifen twice in the head before fleeing. Ms. Zhang was seriously injured and has been sent to the hospital. The murderers have not been caught, and the motive for the crime is also unknown.

Wuxi 82

The Tongyu Su-Li Liner Stops Operating. The Su-Li cargo liner of the Liangxi Road Tongyu Wheel Bureau has been reported by fellow colleagues Lao Gong, Maotai Chang, Xiexing, Ruishengxiang and other wheel transport companies for violating departmental regulations, and they have requested the County Construction Bureau to forward the request to the Construction Department to investigate and revoke the license and verify whether there is a Su-Li route. Yesterday, the county government received instructions from the Construction Department to forward the order to the Tongyu Wheel Bureau to stop operating immediately and await verification and handling.

Positive Efforts to Demolish the South Moon City. The South Moon City in this county is obstructing traffic, and local people have repeatedly requested the Construction Bureau to demolish it. Therefore, Yao Dixing, the director of the Construction Bureau, prepared a plan and submitted it to the county government to be forwarded to the provincial government for review and handling. Recently, the provincial government's meeting resolved to approve it and instructed County Magistrate Pan to forward the order to the Construction Bureau. After receiving the order, Director Yao immediately ordered the Municipal Engineering Office to hire workers on the 20th of this month to start the demolition and complete it within 30 days.

Changzhou 83

The Suspension of Business in Restaurants is Still Difficult to Resolve. The restaurant industry in Wuyi County has been ordered by the levy office to collect customers' donations for banquets, and they are dissatisfied with this procedure. They have unanimously suspended business since the 12th and have requested assistance from all sectors of society. The county government meeting discussed the matter on the morning of the same day and decided that the Public Security Bureau would convene a meeting of all relevant parties to discuss a solution, but no results were achieved. After the representatives of the restaurants returned to the association, they discussed ways to cope with the situation and put forward six conditions, including the direct collection of banquet fees by the levy office. Therefore, it is not easy to resolve the matter for a while, and the strike continued on the 13th.

Business Tax Survey. Wan Bingduan, commissioned by the Jiangsu Provincial Department of Finance, has come to Changzhou as the director of business tax to handle all matters in conjunction with the Finance Bureau. A letter was sent to the Chamber of Commerce a few days ago requesting an investigation into the number of business households in the territory and an estimate of how many there are. The Chamber of Commerce has never had accurate statistics on the number of business households in the territory. The Chamber of Commerce estimated that there are about 20,000 households and replied to the Finance Bureau accordingly.

The District Chief Training Class Holds Graduation. The Jiangsu Provincial District Chief Training Class held its graduation examination the day before yesterday. Recently, the head of the education department of the training class plans to invite the head of the provincial government and various committee members to the class for instruction before the students leave the class in order to expand the students' academic abilities. The Department of Civil Affairs has reported to the provincial government for approval and has agreed on the dates for the chairman and various committee members to come to the class for instruction. The dates are as follows: January 12, Provincial Government Committee Member Sun Hongzhe; 13th, Committee Member He Yushu; 14th, Chairman Ye Chucang; 15th, Committee Member Chen Hexian; 16th, Committee Member Hu Pu'an; 17th, Committee Member Li Mingyang; 19th, Committee Member Chen Qicai. All are scheduled for 2:00 p.m. The class plans to hold a graduation ceremony on the 20th after the various committee members have given their instructions.

The Highway Bureau Purchases Portable Railroads. The Jiangsu Provincial Highway Bureau plans to set up portable railroads along the provincial highways in order to quickly complete the provincial highway and facilitate the transportation of engineering materials. It has recently been reported that there are many such portable railroads and loading railroad cars stored in the Wuhu and Hankou mines. Assistant Engineer Zhang Jingcheng has been specially sent to purchase them for use.

The Department of Finance Appoints Ten District Inspectors. Chen, the director of the Department of Finance, has appointed inspectors to inspect the finances of each county in the province. He has divided the counties of the province into ten districts and appointed inspectors to go to inspect them separately. After being appointed, the members have already set out to inspect.

Gu Baxiang of Quan Gongting Kidnapped Quan Gongting, an important town in Dongxiang, was approached by two bandit boats at around 6 PM on the 10th, carrying forty to fifty bandits led by the notorious bandits Liu Dexing and Cheng Laohu. They deployed sentries along the way. Seeing this, merchants in the town closed their doors one after another, fortunately without disturbing the merchants. Ningbo 90

Municipal Government Ordered to Abolish Village and Li Committees The Ningbo Municipal Government was ordered to abolish the village and li committees because it did not comply with the Municipal Government Organization Law, wasted public funds, and achieved no results. It repeatedly petitioned the provincial government and the central government for abolishment to reduce the burden on citizens. However, the central government, considering the special circumstances of Ningbo, did not approve the abolishment. Because the suffering of citizens could not be alleviated as long as the municipal government was not abolished, it continued the movement to abolish the city in December of last year, jointly petitioning the provincial government to dissolve the city. It is now learned that the provincial government approved the abolishment of the Ningbo Municipal Government at the 366th provincial affairs meeting, to be taken over by the Yin County Government, and ordered the municipal government to complete the closure before the 15th of this month.

News of Changes to Yin County Magistrate Yin County Magistrate Chen Baolin has been in office for more than three years and has achieved excellent results. Robbers Rob and Kill Two People In Chen Xiaodong's home in Chen Tanghui, Shinan Village, Naxiang, Yin County, four bandits suddenly arrived on the evening of the other day.

When Chen heard the alarm, he shouted "Catch the thief!" His sister-in-law, Chen Zhou, responded and came out. The bandits shot and killed Chen Zhou and Chen. Fearing arrest, the bandits fled in panic.

Public Security Bureau to be Changed to Police Department The Ningbo Municipal Public Security Bureau, formerly known as the Ningbo Police Department, used to have broad jurisdiction over the police affairs of various townships in Yin County before the city and county were separated. After the establishment of the municipal government, the city and county were governed separately, and it was renamed the Ningbo Municipal Public Security Bureau. According to reliable provincial sources, after the provincial government abolishes the Ningbo Municipality, considering Ningbo's importance as a major trading port and the extreme importance of public security, it plans to merge the municipal and county public security bureaus and rename it the Ningbo Trading Port Police Department. It will also adopt the organizational structure of the Capital Police Department, renaming the district offices as the First Bureau, Second Bureau, etc., for unified command. The position of the department head will also be re-appointed by the provincial government, directly under the provincial government.

Unexpectedly, Dong suddenly came with her brother on the 22nd, and the wedding was hastily completed the next day. After the marriage, Dong disliked Ma's poverty, and quarrels were frequent within half a month. Then, Ma returned to his hometown on the 14th of last month to visit his family, leaving Dong at the office. When he returned, Dong had fallen in love with Zhu Jing, the county government's radio operator. Seeing Ma, she urgently asked to be divorced, which he angrily agreed to. Educational News

Important News

National Central University's First Memorial Week This Year, Zhu Jiahua Reports on School Affairs 93

Explaining the Purpose of Changing the Academy Deans and Establishing Five Groups

Central University held the first Sun Yat-sen Memorial Week of this year at Boming Hall at 11 AM on the 12th. More than 500 faculty, staff, and students attended. The meeting was presided over by President Zhu Jiahua. The chairman's report stated briefly: "Since I arrived at the school, this is the first time I have attended the Memorial Week. When I took office, it coincided with the beginning of the annual holidays, and I did not have many opportunities to meet everyone. Today, I would like to take this opportunity to give a brief report on the aspects of the school that should be reported to everyone. (1) The administrative organization of our school has always been slightly different from that of other universities in China. It is roughly divided into two departments: academic affairs and general affairs. On the one hand, there is the Academic Council, and on the other hand, there is the Academic Affairs Meeting. Similarly, on the one hand, there is the General Affairs Office or Administrative Office, and on the other hand, there is the Academic Affairs Office. Since the promulgation of the University Regulations, the organization of various schools must be changed. Our school has established three departments: Secretariat, Administrative Affairs, and Academic Affairs, each with a director. Although the University Regulations do not explicitly stipulate how many departments should be established, it seems from the regulations that Academic Affairs and Administrative Affairs can be integrated and need not be separated. Former President Zhang merged the three departments and changed them to a General Affairs Office, which is not different from the original intention of the admission organization regulations. In fact, 'administrative affairs arise from academic affairs and need not be separated and independent from administrative affairs.' Therefore, administrative affairs should be simplified as much as possible and should not be overemphasized. Even the former five offices need not be independent. Therefore, school affairs are handled by five groups: Registration, Documentation, Publication, General Affairs, and Accounting. This is sufficient to increase efficiency and save administrative expenses. In the future, a secretary-general will be added to complete the organization. This plan was decided before I took office and was not based on the request of anyone. A few days ago, I saw a news report saying that it was suggested by students of our school, which is completely untrue. However, some students did ask me about the administrative organization of our school, and I told them my decision. I hope that all students will work hard on academics. I will be responsible for the development of the school. As for the appointments of each group, they have now been hired and are all people with in-depth education, rich knowledge, and the ability to handle affairs. They also do not hold other positions and have their own expertise. Things will naturally go smoothly. (2) Some of the deans of the academies have already resigned to President Zhang. Although I have repeatedly tried to retain them, they cannot dismiss their intention due to various reasons, and some have been resigning for a long time and have left. I had no choice but to hire others. I have now hired Mr. Guo Xinsong to act as the dean of the Law School, and Mr. Zhuang Zexuan to act as the dean of the Education School. Dean Chen Maojie of the College of Engineering had already resigned several times, but I repeatedly asked him to stay, and he has agreed to temporarily continue to be responsible before the appointment of a successor. Dean Bu Bingwen of the College of Agriculture resigned and went to Shanghai because he could not separate himself from his duties in Shanghai. Now, I have invited Gu Xiyu to succeed him. Each of the other colleges has different changes of which the various deans are all well-known scholars with profound knowledge, and I think everyone knows that. (3) There is one more point to report, which is about the issue of funding. Of course, this is a matter of great concern to everyone. The Ministry of Finance and Jiangsu Province have always allocated funds to our school, and the funds are disbursed earlier than to other agencies. The outstanding funds are not much, which shows the government's sincerity in maintaining education. However, our school owes a lot due to construction and other equipment, perhaps several hundred thousand. Because the handover of the previous administration has not been completed, it is not very clear. The first step is to sort out the debts, and then all the construction can be planned and gradually carried out. Today, I will first talk to you about the above points, and there will be many opportunities to meet in the future. I will report everything in the school to everyone at any time."

200 Guests, Chairman Huang Jianzhong

Local News

Graduates of Unregistered Private Schools Must Not Be Employed as Elementary School Teachers Without Examination 99

China Education and Culture Foundation 100

Funds Peking University's Innovation Program

Giving 1 Million Yuan Over Five Years, Peking University Also Contributes 1 Million Yuan

The Board of Directors of the China Education and Culture Foundation held its fifth regular meeting in Shanghai on January 9th. The details of the meeting were seen in the newspapers the other day. Today, the Honorary Secretary of the Foundation, Mr. Hu Shih, gave a speech, revealing that among the motions of the meeting was a case to donate 200,000 yuan annually to Peking University for a period of five years, specifically for the purpose of hiring research chairs and special professors, which is the most important event in domestic higher education in recent years. The following is a record of Mr. Hu's speech. At this meeting, the American director, Mr. Gu Lin, proposed that the Foundation contribute 200,000 yuan annually from the fiscal year of the 20th year of the Republic to the National Peking University for a period of five years, specifically for the establishment of research chairs and special professorships. The conditions and purpose are as follows:

(1) The Foundation and Peking University will each contribute 200,000 yuan annually, for a total of 400,000 yuan, as a special fund for a period of five years.

(2) The uses of this fund are five: (A) Establishment of research chairs, each with an annual salary of 6,000 to 9,000 yuan; (B) Establishment of special professorships, each with an annual salary of 4,800 to 6,000 yuan; (C) Each chair and professorship is accompanied by a corresponding book equipment fee; (D) Establishment of scholarships to assist hardworking and talented students; (E) Establishment of scholarships to reward students who have achieved success in research for advanced research at home or abroad.

(3) The above-mentioned research chairs and special professors must devote themselves to academic research and guide students in academic research, and must not hold any paid or unpaid teaching or administrative duties outside the school. After the new president of Peking University, Mr. Jiang Menglin, agreed to the motion, he submitted it to the fifth regular meeting of the Foundation. Director Jiang requested to recuse himself to avoid suspicion. After a long discussion, the following motion was unanimously passed: "The proposal to cooperate with Peking University to establish research chairs and special professorships is approved in principle, and the Executive Committee of the Foundation will negotiate with the President of Peking University to formulate detailed measures and contract clauses and submit them to the next annual meeting for formal decision." The intention of the above cooperation method is to designate a university with historical significance to pilot a fundamental remedy for university education. Today's university education has three major difficulties: 1. The salaries of professors are too low. The monthly salary of a professor at a national university is not as high as that of a section chief in the government. The highest monthly salary of a professor at Peking University is only 300 yuan, so everyone is doing side jobs to support themselves. 2. The funding for schools is not fixed. Poor scholars do not dare to rely on the salary of a school for a living. 3. Seventy to eighty percent of the school's funding is used for salaries, leaving no money to purchase books and equipment. Therefore, even if there are specialists, they cannot concentrate on advanced academic research. The above method is intended to raise professors' salaries, guarantee the stability of funding, and fully expand the equipment of books and instruments. With one move, all three difficulties can be resolved.

According to the estimation of the original proposer, after this case is established,

Nine research chairs with an average annual salary of 7,000 yuan can be established,

Fifteen special professors with an average annual salary of 5,400 yuan,

Fifteen scholarships of 200 yuan per year,

Fifteen scholarships of 600 yuan per year,

Twelve scholarships of 10,000 yuan per year for graduate students studying abroad,

The above five items total about 176,000 yuan.

The remaining 200,000 yuan will be used to purchase books and equipment and reorganize libraries and laboratories. Over five years, a total of 2 million yuan will be dedicated to improving academic research. Although the pilot project is limited to Peking University, its influence will surely awaken universities across the country to catch up and compete with Peking University in academic pursuits. This can be asserted.

Ministry of Education Orders Shanghai Municipal Education Bureau

The Shanghai Municipal Education Bureau submitted a request to the Ministry of Education to inquire whether to ban graduates of unregistered private schools from serving as teachers in municipal schools. After the Ministry of Education received the report, it instructed the bureau yesterday (12th): "It is understood that Shanghai and its nearby areas have a large number of graduates from normal schools. The selection of teachers for elementary schools should be based on those who are qualified. Graduates of unregistered private schools must not be employed as elementary school teachers unless they have passed the examination. Those who have been approved for registration by the bureau but have not been formally examined should be inspected and identified at any time. Those who have not been registered should not be registered again in order to emphasize the qualifications of teachers and prevent abuses. This order."

Ministry of Education's Attitude Toward the Student Unrest at the Private Anhui High School in Shanghai 101

The Shanghai Private Anhui High School experienced a student unrest. The Shanghai Education Bureau sent personnel to investigate the truth and submitted it to the Ministry of Education for review. After the Ministry of Education received the report, it instructed the Municipal Education Bureau yesterday: "It is understood that the Shanghai Private Anhui High School experienced a strike, and reactionary words were found in leaflets and newspapers. It is said that it was caused by a group of teachers and students colluding with each other. The school has expelled Xu Meishou and other students who caused trouble. The students gathered to the school to destroy it, which is extremely illegal. Since Xu Meishou has been arrested, he should be brought to justice for interrogation. The Public Security Bureau should be transferred to pay attention to the actions of the teachers and students who instigated the unrest in the school at any time to avoid further incidents. However, after investigating the report of the school principal Li Zhenya on the cause of the unrest, he only said that a small number of ambitious teachers directed a small number of students to organize a revolutionary student association in the school, post reactionary slogans, and organize a strike committee to welcome representatives of the Shanghai Revolutionary Student Union to the school to openly preach and coerce a strike. What excuse did the teachers and students use to stir up the unrest? The school principal did not mention it in the report and completely attributed the responsibility for the unrest to others. Based on the meaning of self-reflection, he is too negligent and the report lacks detailed facts. According to the investigators sent by the bureau, the teachers of the school claimed that the students pointed out that the school's equipment was inadequate, and that instruments and books were missing. The current principal is purchasing them. It is clear that the cause of the unrest in the school is also there. Teaching instruments such as books and instruments must not be lacking and should be prepared at the beginning of the opening. Even if the unrest has another background, it is undeniable that the school is poorly managed. The Ministry believes that dealing with the unrest is one matter, and rectifying the school is another matter. The teachers and students who instigated the unrest must not be leniently tolerated, and the school with derelict school affairs must not be allowed to be tolerated. The Shanghai Private Anhui High School has not been filed with the Ministry. If the management situation is like this, the principal should bear the responsibility. The bureau should investigate the situation of the school. If it is simple, corrupt, and difficult to rectify, it should be ordered to close down to avoid misleading the youth and emphasizing education. The handling situation should be reported."
